Oriental Floral fragrance for women and men. <b>Les Sables Roses</b> was launched in 2019. The nose behind this fragrance is Jacques Cavallier Belletrud. </p><div v-pre class='fragrantica-blockquote'><p>Following Ombre Nomade, the house of Louis Vuitton presents the new exclusive edition from the Les Parfums Louis Vuitton line inspired by the Middle East - Les Sables Rose. </p>

<p>"A timeless fragrance trail of rose and oud wood to taste the infinite desert. The desert possesses a singular magic that captivates travelers. At dawn, the sun’s first rays blend the dunes and the sky, night and day, and the earth and clouds into a majestic pink. Fascinated by the harmony that springs from contrasts, the Master Perfumer Jacques Cavallier Belletrud has composed a hot and cold perfume playing with two exceptional qualities of rose and oud. Its simple, limpid script underscores the natural beauty and richness of two of perfumery’s most legendary ingredients. The freshness of rose and the woody depths of oud exalt one another, borne aloft by a warm swirl of ambergris."</p>

<p>Louis Vuitton Les Sables Roses is available as a 100 and 200 ml Eau de Parfum.</p></div><p class="reviewstrigger" style="font-size: smaller; color: #83a6c4">Read about this perfume in other data-tabs-content="deeplinked-tabs"><div class="tabs-panel is-active" id="all-reviews"><div class="cell">
    <div class="strike-title"><span>All Reviews By Date</span></div>
    <div class="grid-x grid-padding-x grid-margin-y" style="position: relative; padding: 0 0.25rem 0 0.25rem;">
        <div class="cell destinationreview"></div>                    <div id="parent2313559" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2313559" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="BLACKZEORANGER"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2004633"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="BLACKZEORANGER" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2313559ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2313559" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.85); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2004633">BLACKZEORANGER</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-12">10/12/24 14:10</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Les Sables Roses is rose rose rose. It’s not a super jammy rose but it isn’t super dry or powdery. I do get the oud and it helps balance the rose that’s in this but don’t be fooled this is absolutely a ROSE fragrance. You can’t compare it to ombré nomads. I have both and they are not the same. <br />
<br />
The closest fragrance you can compare this to is Initio’s Atomic Rose. Both are sexy. Atomic Rose is sweeter but Les Sables Roses is airy on the skin. Don’t smell it up close but ask the people around you how they feel about it. I’ve been told that it smells heavenly on my skin. It definitely lasts it just isn’t as dense as Ombré Nomade.<br />
<br />
As a man I love rose and this does just enough to not be too feminine. However wear fragrances because you like it. I prefer this over Ombré Nomade because I can layer it with more fragrances. And I hate to say it but more people enjoy smelling this than ombré nomade. It’s less offensive. If you have the money, buy both. If you want a sweeter more playful fragrance then go with Atomic Rose.<br />
<br />
9/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55040"comment_id="2313559"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Les-Sables-Roses-55040.html?ccid=2313559#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2293905" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1758544">chaosepher</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-01">03/01/24 00:03</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>LSR<br />
<br />
One thing i don't hear often enough is the way this perfumer J.C. makes this "watery accord" i feel it in most of his creations.<br />
LSR is for me a vast landscape and stillness of mind  luxury and calmness<br />
A clean rose smell which is simply pleasant, its not overly jammy or sweet.<br />
it has this feeling as if you are in a flower shop that specializes in rose and you smell the roses and the water misted on them<br />
As a big room, or rather a wide open place<br />
<br />
I have read the description on the LV website and i instantly agreed with the image of a desert with an oasis, a sort fantasy place<br />
<br />
Its said that this is a counter part to Ombre Nomade and i totally see this. While ON is like more masculline twilight or night in this vast desert LSR is the sunrise, crispness of morning, hope, elevation. (i think both are unisex however LSR may appear more feminine leaning due to the emphasis on rose)<br />
<br />
I don't get much oud in this, however i feel that the oud and sort of pepper note is there to create the sense of space and oriental feel. <br />
<br />
Perfomance is nice i get around 7-9 hours that i can smell it clearly around me it sorts of dance around me with this airy comforting quality. If you smell it up close it gives impression of soap (which i find nice) . In the air its that lovely watery vibe as if there is water nearby or as if you are in a humid place i.e. taking a bath in a steamy bathroom.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1705078">akshat_dudeja</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-01-20">01/20/24 04:41</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Wore this at the club and even though I got loads of compliments on it especially from the ladies, a few even said I smelled like a p!mp but in a sexy way lol. The performance is nice, not as good as the Ombre Nomade though. This one lowkey smells better than Ombre Nomade and is definitely much more versatile. Ombre Nomade might smell a little dirty to people at times, but not this one. IMHO this has everything i was looking for in the Ombre Nomade which it lacked. This one is more rounded off, more seductive(the seduction factor on this is way beyond other perfumes, especially if you dress expensive too but preferably not loud luxury), and is may be more dominant than Ombre Nomade. Ombre Nomade smells like it's a wannabe for power and attention, whereas Les Sables Roses smells like an already well established powerful and influential person. Men might perceive it as just another floral fragrance if they smell it on a woman, but if a man wears this, it works wonders, men especially need to grab a bottle of this one asap.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1341217">Yolis</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-01-16">01/16/24 18:34</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>On initial application it's Bulgarian Rose + Saffron mainly. The oud takes a minute to settle and come out, with the ambergris lightly following. The saffron fades into the background. This smells elegant, but to me the oud isn't as intense as something like Oud Satin Mood, where the oud is super baby wipe like, or even Velvet Rose + Oud, where the oud is deep and nutty almost reminiscent of a gourmand. Les Sables Rose is less in your face than those scents however. Somehow smells soft and clean as well. It's a good post bath evening perfume. The oud makes this fragrance lean a little powdery.<br />
<br />
Definitely unisex. Super well blended.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55040"comment_id="2033093"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Les-Sables-Roses-55040.html?ccid=2033093#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2030842" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1733487">JusttheFactsMan</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-11-28">11/28/23 09:13</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>#450 in my "Tour de Fragrance"<br />
<br />
I avoid rose fragrances on the whole because of the curse of the "grandma scent."  At first the oud is so powerful that it overwhelms the rose, but as it dries down this becomes more rosey. Not Avon "To a Wild Rose" great-grandma rosey, but too grandma rosey for me. Well left of unisex. This is absolutely not car pool, elevator or office safe, unless you're that past-retirement-age librarian that doesn't want members of the public coming anywhere near you and the check-out counter. Definitely a cold weather only choice. Lasts 4-5 hours, though sillage isn't more than moderate to my nose. A date scent only for committed celibates. This is one you'd only wear for your own enjoyment, and I don't enjoy it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55040"comment_id="1987311"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Les-Sables-Roses-55040.html?ccid=1987311#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1983209" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1983209" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="blindboughtjunkie"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1310923"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1310923.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="blindboughtjunkie" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/DS-Durga/Debaser-29736.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.29736.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Debaser"title="Debaser"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1983209ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1983209" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.7); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1310923">blindboughtjunkie</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-11-23">11/23/23 01:58</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This one REALLY grew on me. Now I can't stop dousing myself in this. <br />
<br />
For some context, I am not typically a fan of most ouds out there, or plain rose scents. A friend prompted me to try it and I was extremely doubtful at first. It smelled like this old rose-scented talcum powder from my childhood that I hated, but something about it kept me going back to the store for sprays. <br />
<br />
What made it click was a sample card I kept in my key clès for a week. Every time I opened my purse, I was hit with a mysterious and seductive, rosy, almost leathery scent. It's both dark and uplifting, which makes sense given the "hot and cold" juxtaposition that the perfumer intended. I couldn't stop thinking about it and gave in. <br />
<br />
I would describe it as a dry, yet crisp and crunchy rose. I struggle to smell oud in this (maybe because of how it is not sweet at all, and doesn't bring out the oud in the way most "rose oud vanilla" fragrances do, iykwim). Think the rose in Delina without the fruit and sweetness. On me, it actually comes off as light rosewater and I can wear it in the office :D<br />
<br />
The scent on a beautiful leather-clad woman strutting down the street or getting off a motorcycle -- that is Les Sables Roses.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55040"comment_id="1983209"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Les-Sables-Roses-55040.html?ccid=1983209#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1980768" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1894161" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="tanaC"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/75237"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.75237.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="tanaC" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1894161ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1894161" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.88); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/75237">tanaC</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-08-04">08/04/23 10:42</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Les Sables Roses<br />
<br />
Les Sables Roses (for short LSR) is beautiful dark-red rose scent offering from the house LV, I was thinking something more challenging or dense Rose/Oud fragrance after successful on Ombre Nomade (for short OB), but LSR is another story.<br />
<br />
This is fairy thin and airy, even I bit transparent than  powdery offering like Rose des Vents, however the beautifulness lays in polite spicy (mildly cooling safforn) with Airy dew yet dense Rose. It is mildy boozy / with sweet honey undertone with might come from the rose itself.<br />
<br />
The oud is much tame even more than Oud Wood, I struggle to notice any Oud in this but it do had some woody aspect inside.<br />
<br />
This is nothing ground breaking or innovate but it is the scents done well as usual from LV.<br />
<br />
I would struggle a bit to offer something like this on daily basis but It is ok for all box, except slightly higher price that I bring overall score down.<br />
<br />
8/10 as first impression.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55040"comment_id="1894161"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Les-Sables-Roses-55040.html?ccid=1894161#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1891809" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1461073">jjluvsm9</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-03-25">03/25/23 05:34</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The rose here isn’t especially jammy on my skin, it’s somehow in between fresh and jammy, having a bit of a translucent quality (I notice this running theme with the LV fragrances in general actually). This perfume is 70% that type of rose and 30% oud and musk. Far into the drydown you get the beauty of saffron peaking through which is when the fragrance feels most elevated, in my opinion. I wish the saffron was amped up from the get go, it would’ve added some much needed character to this scent. As much as it’s a lovely scent that is very well done, it’s been done a thousand times before and I’m not entirely convinced, as I also feel with Ombre Nomade, the composition justifies the price tag. I just feel myself wanting ‘more’. That said, I’ll use up my bottle easily as I find this scent very wearable. All the LV frags are very wearable in fact, even OM despite being the heaviest offering. Cavalier has smoothened out the edges of each perfume to the point that it all feels very wearable and easy. That’s a positive of that style of perfumery, on the other hand you could end up feeling how I feel which is that there is a lack of character to the whole thing.<br />
Tl;dr a solid ROSE-oud scent, but nothing standout about it</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55040"comment_id="1792164"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Les-Sables-Roses-55040.html?ccid=1792164#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1786168" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1046089">mohammad.anas.memon</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-02-24">02/24/23 03:13</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Lately, i have been obsessed with rose scents. That luscious, sexy, sultry being that has all my attention these days. Sorry my dear jasmine, I'm not cheating on you, its just we need to take a break, please? <br />
<br />
Let me just say it beforehand, Les Sables Roses is not a unique scent, it is very expensive and it does not offer a high value for your money. Happy? You may just skip my review right then and there. <br />
<br />
But i would be lying if i say, I don't like this beautiful, beautiful, beautiful scent. Because, i love it. I absolutely love it. Its dark, mysterious, intoxicating, bewildering, alluring, juicy, sensual and many other adjectives I can't think of right now. <br />
Does it have oud? Not to my nose. My nose picks up inky, slightly greenish rose right in the start which turns sweet and full with airiness to it. It does have shades of Ombre Nomad (may be similar rose?) but overall it just doesn't stray away from its line. <br />
<br />
Performance is something, i wish was better. It is good, don't worry but i wish it was as good as Nomad or Imagination. It does last on skin for about 4-5 hours with very subtle, shy projection. You would be enjoying the whiffs but others may not. <br />
<br />
Recommendation? Its very hard to recommend LV fragrances these days considering its retail price and thrashing of our currency. But as i always say, try it and make your decision. If you are into roses, this will be on your shelf soon. If you are not, it still might find a place, if not on your shelf then atleast in your heart.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55040"comment_id="1768021"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Les-Sables-Roses-55040.html?ccid=1768021#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1737192" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1371398">teh</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-05-15">05/15/22 11:24</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Very different approach from Ombre Nomade or Nuit De Feu! This is a realistic rose bouquet at the top that gets slightly sweeter toward the heart and then dries down to a really pleasant aquatic woody-musky base. I couldn’t detect any sharp synthetic ambroxan but something in the sillage keeps telling me that it’s there, especially in the dry down. The entire experience on my skin is nothing but extremely pleasant and uplifting - I don’t think this would ever offend anyone. There isn’t much oud, at least to my nose, not much spices either. I appreciate the fact that the rose notes in here aren’t powdery, obnoxious, or just aren’t trying too hard to impress like most other rose-oud fragrances. Les Sables Roses feels really effortless, elegant, low-key, and stylish, which really vibes with me and deserves a spot in my collection.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; When they smell it on me.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55040"comment_id="1557086"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Les-Sables-Roses-55040.html?ccid=1557086#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1554802" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1554802" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="OneGoodScent"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1486126"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="OneGoodScent" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Les-Sables-Roses-55040.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.55040.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Les Sables Roses"title="Les Sables Roses"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1554802ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1554802" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.84); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1486126">OneGoodScent</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-05-01">05/01/22 14:06</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The problem with writing this review is that I have so so much to say about not only this fragrance, but Louis Vuitton parfums in general. This fragrance is a home run for me, me being the key word.<br />
<br />
I’m not going to make any ground breaking comparisons in this review like most other people’s review. It’s expensive! Over priced? That’s for you to judge and value is in the eye of the beholder. My mother always says “everyone knows the price, but very few know the value”. This rings true for this parfum. I do not regret my purchase and I absolutely love Louis Vuitton’s refil program. There is so much waste in the world and it’s nice to make a simple, beautiful bottle last. So chapeau to LV.<br />
<br />
The bottle’s from LV are a beautiful statement. Minimalistic, elegant, charming. It holds well in the hand and looks very sharp. LV got this down and they really shouldn’t be making much, if any changes to their bottles. As well, extra praise should be given to the atomiser. This just feels like love and attention was paid to the finished design. <br />
<br />
Now, what about the scent? Glad you asked. I have a bottle and I carefully considered (read: thirst’d for a full year) before I bought. I went in at least 5 times to a LV shop to take in the fragrance. It knocked me back a full foot each time. I was in love with this scent the moment I smelled, but I had a few other scents I wanted to try first before committing. <br />
<br />
This is rosy! A really good rose, but a balanced rose, musk, pepper. It’s bold and wants to stand out. If this fragrance was a person, it would be a 30 year old entrepreneur named Alex. He would run a successful, small chain of hip cafes in New York City that had won the North American barista awards x3 years in a row. Impressive, integrity, charming! You just want to surround yourself with its company and be inspired by the positive vibes. <br />
<br />
The scent lasts and that rose scent lingers for hour after hour. I found the musk dissipates after 5-6 hours but that beautiful rose just hangs out. On my skin, with my pH, this is not bad and I don’t find it a headache at all. Again, I think this comes down to the quality and attention to good ingredients. Currently this is my go to scent. If I was a pimp, this would be my bottom bitch, and she is holding me down.<br />
<br />
Overall, I would highly recommend sampling this scent. Remember, its not shy and it has character. It wants to breathe. I can’t tell you how to spend your money, but I don’t feel it’s over priced. Again, that’s subjective and I understand this concern. <br />
<br />
Packaging: 10/10<br />
Price: 8.5/10<br />
Scent: 10/10<br />
Longevity: 9/10<br />
Sillage: 9/10<br />
<br />
Over all, I would give Les Sable Roses a hard 9/10. LV have got the marketing and packaging down, lock down! It’s really tight and I would be slightly sad to see them make any changes at this point. This scent is wonderful. Refills is such a big selling point for me. Chepeau LV.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55040"comment_id="1554802"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Les-Sables-Roses-55040.html?ccid=1554802#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1553493" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1463044">Warmind77</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-03-26">03/26/22 04:57</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Floating on cloud made of roses just after sunset. That's the image that always gets evoked whenever I apply this perfume. This is an airy yet dense rose perfume with darkness around its edges.<br />
There's realistic warm rose, with more rose. Just the flower, I can't detect any stems or any other greenness here. Of course there's the aloof figure of oud that chaperones every sniff, but the cool kind that's happy to sit back in silence and let the roses have all the fun.<br />
The blend is dark enough to worn by either gender and radiates best in colder months or summer nighttimes. <br />
Don't expect magic tricks, the scent doesn't very little to deceive its opening to offer different scents as time stretches, it stays in the world of rose from start to its very distant finish.<br />
It will stay on skin for some time and projects above average when I've apply 4+ sprays, so be mindful of your environment when you choose this.<br />
It's a beautiful rose perfume with some oud (it's not a typical rose + oud in my view) that's quite linear but it's well made and you can smell there are quality ingredients used here. None of the usual chemical harshness you may get from other rose scents.<br />
Worth the price if you love rose if you value a realistic quality depiction of it; probably not good value if you don't.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55040"comment_id="1530704"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Les-Sables-Roses-55040.html?ccid=1530704#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1527467" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1393012" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="RisingChaos"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1352837"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1352837.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="RisingChaos" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1393012ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1393012" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.74); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1352837">RisingChaos</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2021-08-15">08/15/21 22:59</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>It's a slightly spicy rose and oud combo, floral and a bit of dirty/earthy woods, with a sort of mentholic lift that comes across as airy and clean. To me, this falls right in between MFK's Oud Satin Mood EDP and its Extrait. Where Satin Extrait takes the rose-oud of the EDP and balances it heavily toward rose while adding spice, LSR basically adds the spice while maintaining a more even balance of rose and oud. That gentle dusting of spice adds a slight fuzziness or powderyness that really elevates the rose + oud to another level of sensuality but where Satin Extrait has a soft and warm cinnamon that complements the sexy factor, LSR has harsh and uninviting black pepper that kinda takes away from it a bit.<br />
<br />
Performance is similarly nuclear. I get 5-6hr of powerful projection and 16hr+ longevity. Satin Mood Extrait just edges it out ever-so-slightly for me, as cinnamon is definitely an upgrade over black pepper plus I prefer the more heavy rose anyway, but LSR is still a dark, seductive, high-performance rose-oud in its own right.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1363509" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Chesco"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1249347"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1249347.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Chesco" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Tom-Ford/Soleil-de-Feu-80083.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.80083.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Soleil de Feu"title="Soleil de Feu"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1363509ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1363509" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1249347">Chesco</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2021-06-21">06/21/21 09:15</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Rose Oil + White Vanillin + Soap + Commercial Farmed Oud (same found in Ombre Nomad) + Potpourri mixture of other Floral Oils + Ambergris + Saffron + smoky Incense + Black Pepper + Amber+  Basil/Patchouli + something acidic in the end dryoff possibly Benzoin + other small traces of ingredients that my nose can't identify<br />
<br />
This is a Sweet Spicy Soapy Rose dna.<br />
My favorite of all the female frags the LV store had, took me forever to test them all, men's &amp; female's.  But a caveat i have with it is that it gives off the scent of old fashion bath oil rounds, and because of that it gives off a mature woman vibe to it's scent, and yet the sweetness pulls it back to a woman of class in her mid 20's.<br />
There is a small note of Ambergris in the mid dry-off that comes into play, giving it a unique smelling &amp; sea airiness note, and makes the dna elegant. The Oud in here is done with just a drop to give the fragrance depth and richness which also modernizes the dated Rose/Soap scent.  The Oud note is a supporting backbone to the dna, not funky and will be undetectable to bystanders. <br />
Love the frag, it projects strongly and leaves an huge scent trail.  <br />
This is a very strong &amp; long lasting fragrance!<br />
But, it's dna is a bit dated, and some smelling the strong whiffs over &amp; over throughout the day may run the risk of finding this cloying.  Some females i have given samples to have replied that at times it's headache inducing.  So go get yourself a free tester at the store and try on your skin first before buying a bottle.<br />
Fantastic performance, last hours.<br />
This is absolutely feminine, and unless you are gay, i would absolutely only recommend this frag for the ladies.  The Men's offering 'Ombre Nomad' is masculine and has a fabulous opening &amp; mid.  This scent also gives me a vibe that a person can get tired of smelling this everyday.<br />
They sell a 200ml size bottle that works out to be the cheapest per ml.<br />
I prefer Armani's 'Roses D'Arabie more, as the Oud is a enjoyable higher quality.<br />
<br />
4/5 Woofs!<br />
<br />
------<br />
<br />
WARNING! BAIT &amp; SWITCH SCAM BY LV:<br />
<br />
The best quality juice of this frag is the free sample that comes in it's own little box packaging that is the highest quality of oily juice that sticks to the skin and leaves a beautiful shine on your arm that makes you feel like you're wearing quality which makes you smell like young money and sexy af, but is really a 'bait &amp; switch' to scam the customer, because:<br />
<br />
The store tester is slightly watered down.<br />
The juice in the bottle is noticeably more watered down.<br />
The juice in the refill is even more watered down than the bottle.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55040"comment_id="1363509"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Les-Sables-Roses-55040.html?ccid=1363509#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1346165" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I sure do hate that happened because I’m not a fan of this. I must admit that it does smell very high quality for what it is, but it’s not my taste. It’s just so good — a dusty, creamy, mildly sweet but fresh rose. I find the oud disappeared in the dry down, but is very prominent initially.<br />
<br />
Everything about it is so smooth and pleasant. I’m addicted to this scent. Something about this is so nostalgic and familiar in the best way, but I can’t put my finger on what it is, still it makes me happy. Les Sables Roses has made its way into my collection of favourite fragrances of all time.<br />
<br />
Pulled the trigger on a full bottle after using up my 2ml sample in a week, no regrets yet. Personally I think longevity could and really should be better. Sillage and projection are strong for 1-2 hours, then it gets close to skin, but is very much gone by 12 hours (on skin, haven’t tested on clothes). However, I only wear 2-3 sprays of this each time as I have to use sparingly, maybe if I sprayed some more it might improve the performance, idk tho. We all need a couple in our collections! <br />
I am on a rose-train, trying out a lot of them theese days. And i have found a few really good..<br />
<br />
So what about Les Sables Roses?<br />
This has a bright, crystal clear rose in the opening. It´s great, for sure. <br />
Oud and ambergris is soft and tuned down, this is not offensive or fecal. Don´t get the heavy ambergris some of you are talking about. No problem! <br />
<br />
But but but....longevity? For the grand price Louis Vuitton are asking.... (not asking, really, they just charge you 300 euros and holds up the door as you leave the boutique)....i need better longevity. <br />
So, fantastic rose for 1 hour, and it´s a BEAUTIFUL first hour, trust me, but i want more than that (for that price). <br />
<br />
A fragance i will suggest (instead) is La Fille de Berlin Serge Lutens. There we have a even brighter rose than in Les Sables Roses. <br />
<br />
And if you want a "masculine" dark rose, you could try Garanat from Bvlgari. (A favorite, projection and longevity super de luxe).<br />
<br />
But hey, Les Sables Roses is - to me - a really good rose fragance. I would love to have a full bottle in my collection...if somebody else paid for it.<br />

Its Sits Between Something Like FM Lipstick Rose &amp; Portrait Of A Lady For Me.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55040"comment_id="1209584"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Les-Sables-Roses-55040.html?ccid=1209584#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1209056" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Les Sables Roses clearly is the most elegant, délicate, and féminine among the 3.<br />
No clear préférence here, however, as the uses are different (Sables Roses for mornings, Encens Mythique for afternoon, Satin Mood at bedtime).<br />
The tuning of Ambergris and Oud vs. the bouquet of roses is really fantastic in Sables Roses: each component's expression is just perfect, there is no underdog whatsoever: each time one of the 3 seems to start dominating, the other 2 make their come-back majestically, and the whole game is frankly fascinating.<br />
No idea how much time it took Cavallier to tune this music, but in the end we get a harmonious and impressive olfactive symphony !</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; It transcends gender, it transcends trends, it transcends time. The highest quality ingredients, the most effervescent ambergris, Oud, and rose trail. It’s a stunning fragrance that is wearable everyday in all seasons. But would you really want to? It’s so good that you should probably save it for special occasions. Unlike other highly oriental fragrances, this one doesn’t require the wearer to explain to passersby what they are smelling. It will be appreciated by all noses, regardless of experience. Aventus is considered THE fragrance of pineapple; Les Sables Roses should be considered THE fragrance of rose and wood. But in a way I am happy that it isn’t well known or hyped so that I smell unique.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55040"comment_id="1143923"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Les-Sables-Roses-55040.html?ccid=1143923#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1139080" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1223088">Salama78</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2020-01-28">01/28/20 11:32</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I have a strange experience with performance of Les sables rose.. although it is one of the best performing perfume in my collection,it almost has no smell in the first moment I spray it.. very subtle and shy..but after about ten seconds it starts to shine..I get rose leans to feminine vibe which I am not fond of..but quickly it turns to a creamy smell of oud and ambergris that never becomes jammy nor animalic..in my experience it has no similarity with ombre nomade as it has been suggested.. ombre nomade is totally another domain of oud based fragrance and truly leans musculine which I really like more..Les sables rose is all about rose with a very shy oud.. perhaps it is more favourable to women than men I guess..but by all means it is unisex..I tried it several times to discover what may be under the hoods.. but unfortunately I don't get too much..to me it is just an ordinary rose based fragrance with high price tag of Louis Vuitton.. although I got some good reactions when I wore it,it is still a very unsophisticated smell to my nose..<br />
It has a very good performance though..<br />
That is all..</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55040"comment_id="1139080"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Les-Sables-Roses-55040.html?ccid=1139080#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1104144" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1079916">mongut</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2019-10-05">10/05/19 18:14</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I personally have the opposite order of preference than the previous reviewer.  I prefer Les Sables Roses to Ombre Nomad by a wide margin.  I adore a natural, photorealistic rose note—and it's so hard to get right in fragrances.  Oud, on the other hand, I can appreciate while not personally preferring it.  It's usually too heavy, too intense, too masculine.  Rose and oud together is almost cliche now; HOWEVER, nothing about this masterpiece is cliche.  The oud lingers way in the background at first and becomes more prominent in the dry-down.  For someone who stays away from oud I find Les Sables Roses supremely well balanced in all its notes.  This is a rich, yet effervescent rose fragrance.  My previous favorite rose was Aerin Rose de Grasse, which combines amber and rose to perfection.  Les Sables Roses is more complex, with noticeable amber, rose, oud and even a tiny bit of spice.  Ah-mey-zing!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55040"comment_id="1104144"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Les-Sables-Roses-55040.html?ccid=1104144#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1093895" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:4,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1183164">trillav</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2019-09-03">09/03/19 03:27</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Yes I agree, it is a masterpiece. If you buy any LVs, buy Ombre Nomad (that is in first place) then this. These are the standouts from the line. And by standouts I mean both are in my top 3 of ALL TIME...and I have hundreds of niche / luxury frags.<br />
<br />
I now proudly own a 200ml bottle of this AND a 100ml one. <br />
<br />
To those that say these are nothing special in the oud/rose category....jog on! I totally disagree.<br />
<br />
Both Ombre Nomad and Les Sables Roses are groundbreaking in terms of oud rose scents and done exceptionally well. This is a beautiful rose...deep and dark. Very realistic. Like you have a bouquet of roses sitting right in front of you. Simply stunning. It is my top EVER rose scent in terms of quality, longevity, sillage etc. This smells EXTREMELY expensive...anyone near you will be able to smell this is no high street perfume.<br />
<br />
<br />
Whereas Ombre Nomad is much darker and skankier, this is still dark and heavy but the rose very much is at the forefront which makes this somewhat of a crisper, more feminine scent. It is still heavy but somehow smells "cleaner" than Ombre Nomad if that makes sense. Both are stunning.<br />
<br />
EDIT: After wearing this for 8 hours, it smells similar to Ombre Nomad in the drydown...they both have a kind of salty, rich oud smell.<br />
<br />
If I had to choose only 1....it would be difficult... I would go with Ombre Nomad however if you have the budget for two, this is 100% full bottle worthy.<br />
<br />
WHY is this rated 3.79??? This is a 5/5!!!!<br />
<br />
EDIT: This is in my top 3 of all time. No designer perfume house has come close to touching LV in their perfume releases. This is worth every penny, and I never think that when it comes to high end frags. Most are a rip-off, poor longevity, cheap smelling, etc. But the bottle design, cap, sprayer, sillage, quality of ingredients....these are simply divine.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1554802" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="OneGoodScent"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1486126"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="OneGoodScent" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Les-Sables-Roses-55040.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.55040.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Les Sables Roses"title="Les Sables Roses"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1554802ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1554802" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.78); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1486126">OneGoodScent</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-05-01">05/01/22 14:06</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The problem with writing this review is that I have so so much to say about not only this fragrance, but Louis Vuitton parfums in general. This fragrance is a home run for me, me being the key word.<br />
<br />
I’m not going to make any ground breaking comparisons in this review like most other people’s review. It’s expensive! Over priced? That’s for you to judge and value is in the eye of the beholder. My mother always says “everyone knows the price, but very few know the value”. This rings true for this parfum. I do not regret my purchase and I absolutely love Louis Vuitton’s refil program. There is so much waste in the world and it’s nice to make a simple, beautiful bottle last. So chapeau to LV.<br />
<br />
The bottle’s from LV are a beautiful statement. Minimalistic, elegant, charming. It holds well in the hand and looks very sharp. LV got this down and they really shouldn’t be making much, if any changes to their bottles. As well, extra praise should be given to the atomiser. This just feels like love and attention was paid to the finished design. <br />
<br />
Now, what about the scent? Glad you asked. I have a bottle and I carefully considered (read: thirst’d for a full year) before I bought. I went in at least 5 times to a LV shop to take in the fragrance. It knocked me back a full foot each time. I was in love with this scent the moment I smelled, but I had a few other scents I wanted to try first before committing. <br />
<br />
This is rosy! A really good rose, but a balanced rose, musk, pepper. It’s bold and wants to stand out. If this fragrance was a person, it would be a 30 year old entrepreneur named Alex. He would run a successful, small chain of hip cafes in New York City that had won the North American barista awards x3 years in a row. Impressive, integrity, charming! You just want to surround yourself with its company and be inspired by the positive vibes. <br />
<br />
The scent lasts and that rose scent lingers for hour after hour. I found the musk dissipates after 5-6 hours but that beautiful rose just hangs out. On my skin, with my pH, this is not bad and I don’t find it a headache at all. Again, I think this comes down to the quality and attention to good ingredients. Currently this is my go to scent. If I was a pimp, this would be my bottom bitch, and she is holding me down.<br />
<br />
Overall, I would highly recommend sampling this scent. Remember, its not shy and it has character. It wants to breathe. I can’t tell you how to spend your money, but I don’t feel it’s over priced. Again, that’s subjective and I understand this concern. <br />
<br />
Packaging: 10/10<br />
Price: 8.5/10<br />
Scent: 10/10<br />
Longevity: 9/10<br />
Sillage: 9/10<br />
<br />
Over all, I would give Les Sable Roses a hard 9/10. LV have got the marketing and packaging down, lock down! It’s really tight and I would be slightly sad to see them make any changes at this point. This scent is wonderful. Refills is such a big selling point for me. Chepeau LV.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55040"comment_id="1554802"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Les-Sables-Roses-55040.html?ccid=1554802#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1400260" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1161847">MrBolton</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2021-05-19">05/19/21 20:44</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I finally bought LV Cactus Garden, and they mistakenly sent me two samples of this instead of my requests.<br />
I sure do hate that happened because I’m not a fan of this. I must admit that it does smell very high quality for what it is, but it’s not my taste. It is also very mature smelling, leaning on the edge of old lady. The rose in it is very natural, outright photorealistic, and the oud is fairly smooth. It doesn’t really get too animalic at any point—if at all.<br />
As a guy in his mid-20s, this is very out of place on me. I do, however, appreciate perfumery and can again understand why people would like it.<br />
Performance-wise, it’s an absolute beast. You’ll only need a drop or two to get through your day still have some projection to spare as you go into the night. <br />
I imagine the rich lady villain from 101 Dalmatians wearing this.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55040"comment_id="1346165"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Les-Sables-Roses-55040.html?ccid=1346165#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1927366" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;
